â”‚ Design decision: Should this be a standalone workflow or enhance existing investigation-workflow? User said "create a new introspection workflow" which suggests standalone. Advantages: 1) Clean separation - focused on assumption validation only, 2) Can be invoked independently, 3) Reuses existing introspection phase. The workflow should support TWO context types: conversational (check assumptions from prior conversation) vs implementation (validate if something is implemented correctly).   â”‚

â”‚ Phase flow design: Phase 1 (context-gathering) â†’ main agent gathers conversational context, determines context type (conversational vs implementation), creates context.json. Phase 2 (pre-research-decision) â†’ checkpoint asks user "Do you want pre-codebase research?". Phase 3 (code-researcher-conditional) â†’ if yes, spawn code-researcher subagent; if no, skip. Phase 4 (assumption-generation) â†’ main agent generates 6-9 assumptions based on context type + any research findings. Phase 5 (external-research-conditional) â†’ main agent determines if external docs needed, optionally uses external-research skill. Phase 6 (validation) â†’ spawn code-qa subagent to validate all assumptions.   â”‚

â”‚ Wait, I'm overcomplicating this. Re-reading user requirements: 1) ask user if they want pre-codebase research using code-researcher (OPTIONAL based on response). This is ONE decision point. 2) generate assumptions from prior context OR implementation. 3) optionally use external-research skill. 4) use code-qa to validate. So the flow should be simpler: Phase 1 (context + user question) â†’ Phase 2 (conditional code-researcher) â†’ Phase 3 (assumption generation) â†’ Phase 4 (optional external-research) â†’ Phase 5 (code-qa validation). Actually, phases 2, 3, 4 could potentially be combined since they're sequential.   â”‚

â”‚ Simplification: Looking at existing workflows, phases should be single-purpose. Best design: Phase 1 (context-gathering-and-decision) â†’ Main agent gathers context, uses AskUserQuestion tool for research decision, outputs context.json. Phase 2 (code-researcher-conditional) â†’ If user said yes, spawn code-researcher subagent for codebase exploration, outputs codebase-findings.json. Phase 3 (assumption-generation) â†’ Main agent reads context + any findings, generates 6-9 assumptions, outputs assumptions.json. Phase 4 (assumption-validation) â†’ Spawn code-qa subagent to validate assumptions against codebase, outputs validation-results.json. External-research should be INTEGRATED into assumption-generation phase, not separate, since it's just a tool the main agent might use.   â”‚
